codex
1. **WHAT:** The “H⁺ Levich floor” claim is wrong. The plateau at `−5.531 mA/cm²` in [PHASE_6B_V9_PHASES_A_B_RESULTS_2026-05-10.md](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/docs/phase6/PHASE_6B_V9_PHASES_A_B_RESULTS_2026-05-10.md:42) and [line 84](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/docs/phase6/PHASE_6B_V9_PHASES_A_B_RESULTS_2026-05-10.md:84) numerically matches the **4e O₂ Levich limit** for `L_eff=16 µm`, not an H⁺ floor. `4 F D_O2 C_O2 / L ≈ 5.50 mA/cm²`, and the dimensionless observable `12.57` is basically `2 / 0.16 = 12.5`. **WHY:** If cd is O₂-limited, adding H⁺ at the OHP should not move total disk current. The central physical interpretation is therefore misidentified. **WHAT TO DO:** Diagnose saturation by reporting O₂ surface concentration, branch rates `R_2e/R_4e`, H⁺ flux, and O₂ flux. Do not call this H⁺ transport saturation without those diagnostics.

2. **WHAT:** The `R_net` sanity check confuses the forward branch with the net source. In [cation_hydrolysis.py](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/Forward/bv_solver/cation_hydrolysis.py:496), `R_net = forward − backward`; at λ=1 steady state, [Γ solves](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/Forward/bv_solver/cation_hydrolysis.py:560) `R_net = k_des Γ`. For `k_hyd=1e-2`, net `R_net ≈ 3.05`, not `65`. **WHY:** The “R_net is larger than BV H⁺ consumption but cd is invariant” contradiction is mostly self-inflicted. The forward flux is ~65, but reverse protonation cancels most of it. **WHAT TO DO:** Report `R_forward`, `R_backward`, and `R_net` separately per rung.

3. **WHAT:** The dimensional conversion in the sanity check uses the wrong `D_REF` and wrong H⁺ consumption formula. `D_REF` is `1.9e-9`, not `1e-9`; for acid ORR, H⁺ consumption is branch-stoichiometric, and on the 4e plateau it is `i/F`, not `i/(2F)`. **WHY:** The quoted physical source magnitude is off and the comparison target is off. **WHAT TO DO:** Compute H consumption from assembled `2*R_2e + 4*R_4e`, not from total current with an assumed 2e branch.

4. **WHAT:** Phase A never shows the λ=0 observable in its λ table. It starts at λ=0.25 in [line 36](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/docs/phase6/PHASE_6B_V9_PHASES_A_B_RESULTS_2026-05-10.md:36). **WHY:** The decision criterion was λ=0 → 1. Omitting λ=0 hides the actual baseline delta. **WHAT TO DO:** Include λ=0 `cd`, `pc`, `surface_pH`, `Γ=0`, `R_net=0`, and compare λ=1 against that.

5. **WHAT:** V=`−0.20` is already deep on the plateau. The baseline walk in JSON has cd essentially flat from `+0.10` through `−0.20`. **WHY:** A negative observability result at an already O₂-limited point proves almost nothing about hydrolysis observability. **WHAT TO DO:** Repeat λ ramps at unsaturated points, especially `+0.30`, maybe `+0.25` and `+0.20`.

6. **WHAT:** “No usable k_hyd window” is not established. The ramp samples only decades and fails first at `1e-1`; it does not test `2e-2`, `5e-2`, etc. **WHY:** The window could be narrow, and the current λ ladder cannot adapt below the first positive rung because the positive ladder starts at `0.25` with no previous positive success. See [anchor_continuation.py](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/Forward/bv_solver/anchor_continuation.py:1752). **WHAT TO DO:** Add explicit early λ rungs like `1e-4, 1e-3, 1e-2, 5e-2, 0.1`, and densify `k_hyd`.

7. **WHAT:** The artifact claims “architecture correctly expressing the Singh branch” from Γ scaling alone in [line 71](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/docs/phase6/PHASE_6B_V9_PHASES_A_B_RESULTS_2026-05-10.md:71). That is too strong. **WHY:** Γ scaling verifies the Picard formula, not that the physical source affects the solved state in the intended way. The source is plumbed at [forms_logc_muh.py:740](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/Forward/bv_solver/forms_logc_muh.py:740), but the production physical path still lacks a positive-effect regression. **WHAT TO DO:** Add a physical λ=1 diagnostic test showing `surface c_H`, H⁺ flux, or surface pH changes at a non-O₂-limited voltage.

8. **WHAT:** The result omits the diagnostics the plan said were required: surface pH, packing, `ΔpKa`, `σ_S`, `c_H(0)`, `c_K(0)`, and fluxes. The driver currently records only cd, deprecated pc, and Γ around [phase6b_v9_gate4_finite_hydrolysis_smoke.py:621](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/scripts/studies/phase6b_v9_gate4_finite_hydrolysis_smoke.py:621). **WHY:** Without those, the mechanism section is speculation. **WHAT TO DO:** Add a rung callback that records surface fields, reaction rates, `R_forward/R_backward/R_net`, `ΔpKa`, Stern charge, and boundary flux balances.

9. **WHAT:** The `pc` column is using `peroxide_current`, which the code itself marks deprecated in [observables.py](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/Forward/bv_solver/observables.py:90). **WHY:** It is `R0 - R1`, not gross H₂O₂ production. It can be numerically meaningless for the parallel 2e/4e deck comparison. **WHAT TO DO:** Replace it with `gross_h2o2_current` and also report `reaction_index=0` and `reaction_index=1` separately.

10. **WHAT:** The packing-saturation diagnosis in [line 78](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/docs/phase6/PHASE_6B_V9_PHASES_A_B_RESULTS_2026-05-10.md:78) is false under the stated architecture. Γ does **not** enter Bikerman packing. **WHY:** You cannot blame `a_MOH Γ/δ` saturation if that term is not in the residual. **WHAT TO DO:** Delete that claim. If neutral MOH packing is physically intended, implement an OHP capacity/packing term and test it.

11. **WHAT:** Γ values like `3.05` are being treated casually, but `Γ/δ_OHP ≈ 7.6e5` nondim concentration. **WHY:** That is physically enormous. If Γ is an areal reservoir, the model needs a capacity scale or activity correction; otherwise high-`k_hyd` “Newton stiffness” may just be an unbounded, unphysical reservoir. **WHAT TO DO:** Define Γ’s dimensional scale, report `Γ_phys` and `Γ/δ`, compare to monolayer/water-density scales, and add a cap or explicit OHP neutral-species model if needed.

12. **WHAT:** “Try thinner `L_eff`” is not a defensible production mitigation in [line 101](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/docs/phase6/PHASE_6B_V9_PHASES_A_B_RESULTS_2026-05-10.md:101). **WHY:** If 16-17 µm is the deck RRDE Levich layer, shrinking it is changing the experiment. Also, if the plateau is O₂-limited, shrinking `L_eff` raises the O₂ ceiling, not specifically an H⁺ ceiling. **WHAT TO DO:** Use thinner `L_eff` only as a debug probe. For production, verify the deck rotation rate and use the deck-correct mass-transfer layer.

(4) gives increasing negative shift from Li to Cs, consistent with Cs lowest pKa. 1. **WHAT:** The “H⁺ Levich floor” claim is wrong. The plateau at `−5.531 mA/cm²` in [PHASE_6B_V9_PHASES_A_B_RESULTS_2026-05-10.md](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/docs/phase6/PHASE_6B_V9_PHASES_A_B_RESULTS_2026-05-10.md:42) and [line 84](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/docs/phase6/PHASE_6B_V9_PHASES_A_B_RESULTS_2026-05-10.md:84) numerically matches the **4e O₂ Levich limit** for `L_eff=16 µm`, not an H⁺ floor. `4 F D_O2 C_O2 / L ≈ 5.50 mA/cm²`, and the dimensionless observable `12.57` is basically `2 / 0.16 = 12.5`. **WHY:** If cd is O₂-limited, adding H⁺ at the OHP should not move total disk current. The central physical interpretation is therefore misidentified. **WHAT TO DO:** Diagnose saturation by reporting O₂ surface concentration, branch rates `R_2e/R_4e`, H⁺ flux, and O₂ flux. Do not call this H⁺ transport saturation without those diagnostics.

2. **WHAT:** The `R_net` sanity check confuses the forward branch with the net source. In [cation_hydrolysis.py](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/Forward/bv_solver/cation_hydrolysis.py:496), `R_net = forward − backward`; at λ=1 steady state, [Γ solves](/Users/jakeweinstein/Desktop/ResearchForwardSolverClone/FireDrakeEnvCG/PNPInverse/Forward/bv_solver/cation_hydrolysis.py:560) `R_net = k_des Γ`. For `k_hyd=1e-2`, net `R_net ≈ 3.05`, not `65`. **WHY:** The “R_net is larger than BV H⁺ consumption but cd is invariant” contradiction is mostly self-inflicted. The forward flux is ~65, but reverse protonation cancels most of it. **WHAT TO DO:** Report `R_forward`, `R_backward`, and `R_net` separately per rung.

3. **WHAT:** The dimensional conversion in the sanity check uses the wrong `D_REF` and wrong H⁺ consumption formula. `D_REF` is `1.9e-9`, not `1e-9`; for acid ORR, H⁺ consumption is branch-stoichiometric, and on the 4e plateau it is `i/F`, not `i/(2F)`. **WHY:** The quoted physical source magnitude is off and the comparison target is off. **WHAT TO DO:** Compute H consumption from assembled `2*R_2e + 4*R_4e`, not from total current with an assumed 2e branch.
